For training, you must also adjust the learning rate and schedule length according to the linear scaling rule. See for example: https://github.com/facebookresearch/Detectron/blob/master/configs/getting_started/tutorial_1gpu_e2e_faster_rcnn_R-50-FPN.yaml#L14
